Apastama-Sulbasutra
with the commentaries of Kapardi, Karavinda and Sundararaja


Input by members of the Sansknet project


This GRETIL version has been converted from a custom Devanagari encoding.
Therefore, word boundaries are usually not marked by blanks.
These and other irregularities cannot be standardized at present.


THE TEXT IS NOT PROOF-READ!

The SUTRA TEXT (only) of this GRETIL version has been checked
against the edition by Albert Brk, ZDMG 55 (1901), pp. 578-591.
Despite numerous corrections, the text of the commentaries
is in urgent need of proof-reading!

Extracted sutra text available as a separate file.


REFERENCE SYSTEM according to Brk's edition.
Where required by the commentaries, the sutras were split,
e.g.: âpøus_1.2a, âpøus_1.2b, âpøus_1.2c etc.

tarhi madhayamatçtãyaü vyàkartya pårvàparayoş pradar÷anàrthaü bhaviùyatãti cennaitatyadyevamiùñamabhaviùyattarhi spaùñataraümadhyame tçtãya ityevàvakùyat, na càsau tattathoktavàn /
atha manyase? tadarthamabhayasyàparasminn ityukte 'bhyàsàdanyat, pramàõamaparaü pratãyate, sàmarthyàttatra tçtãye lakùaõaü bhavatviti, naitadapi yuktaü--yadayamàgantvàyàmàbhyàsaş iti

ekavidhàdãnàüabhavanti

na bhaveyuş /
kutaş? saptavidhavàkya÷eùutvàcchutivipratiùedhàcca /
pakùãbhavatãtyàdipucchavidhàyakavàkyasya saptavidhaprakaraõapàñhàttaccheùatvàvagateş /
ki¤caikavidhe pakùàdivibhàgakaraõe vyàyàmamàtratàhàniş vyàyàmamàtrapakùàdikaraõaikavidhatàhàniriti vyàyàmamàtrapakùapucchaikavidhatvavidhàyakayoş ÷rutyorvirodhànnaikavidhàdãnàü pakùàdayo bhaveyuş /
teùàü karaõopadhànàdãni ekavidhaprabhçtãnàmityatra vakùyati /
nanu sapakùapuccheùu vidhàbhyàse 'pacaye ca visaptamakaraõãü puruùasthànãyàü kçtvà viharedityaùñavidhàdyupacayamate ekavidhàdau apacaye 'pisaptadhà vibhàgaü dar÷ayati /
tatpakùapucchavibhàgàrthaü /

tatkathaü teùàü tàni na bhavantãti /
ucyate -- ekavidhaş prathamo 'gniş, taduhavai saptavidhameva cinvãtetyevamàdyorvi ruddhàrthàbhidhàyinyoş÷rutyoşsamucchayàbhàvàdvikalpa evàvakalpate /
tasmàdekavidho và prathamaş saptavidho và prathamaş /
tatra yadaikavidhaş prathamaş prakçti÷va; tadà dvitãyàdyahàreùu ekottarà eva dvividhàdayaş prayoktavyàş /
prakçtibhåtaikavidhe pakùapucchà nàmanàmnànàdekavidhàdãnàü ùaõõàü pakùapucchàni na bhavanti /
saptavidhe tu vidyanta eva /
evamaùñavidhàdãnàü tadvikàratvàtteùu ca vidyanta eva /
yadà saptavidhaş prakçtiş, itare tadvikaràràş tadaikavidhàdayo 'pyaùñavidhavat sapakùapucchà eva bhaveyuş, evaü vidhàpacayoktaş saptavidhavibhàgo 'rthavàn bhaviùyati, tatràtiràtravadvikçterapi kadàcit prathamato 'nuùñhànaü ekavidhasya labhyata eva /
asminnapi pakùe ekottaraniyamo 'styeva /
yadaikavidhaş prakçti /
prathamamàhàraş, tadàsàvapakùapucchàş /
dvitãyàdiùvàhàreùu dvividhàdayo yàvatsaptavidhamapakùapucchà eva /
saptavidhàdayaşsapakùapucchà eva /
yadaikavidho vikçtiş prathamàhàraş, tadàsau sapakùapucchaş /
dvitã yàdiùvàhàreùu dvividhàdayaşsarve sapakùapucchà eva /
yadà saptavidhaş prakçtirvà vikçtirvà prathamaş, tadà tata årdhvamaùñavidhàdayaşsaptavidhà eva /
tasmàdekavidhàdãnàü ùaõõàmapakùapucchatvaü sapakùapuvchatvamubhayamapyastyeveti sarvamupapannam /
aùñavidhàdiùvekottareùu kathamatiriktasya vibhàga ityata àha --

aùñavi yeta

asyàrthaş -- aùñavidhàdiùvardhàùñamebhyo yadanyadadhikamàgantu tatsaptadhà saptàrdhadhà vibhajya pratipuruùaü -- puruùe ùuruùe bhàgamekaikamàve÷ayet /

apareõa yåpàvañade÷aü saücaramava÷iùyetyàdi vimàya pakùàpyayeùu ÷aïkuü nihatya dakùiõottarayà rajjvà navàratnãn pràde÷amaïgulaü caturbhàgonàü càyàmaü kçtvà pakùàgreùu ÷aïkuü nihanyàt /
